Important News

Self-Defense Army

Yang's Troops Attack Acheng Again

Fierce battle with Japanese troops on the 6th

Ma Zhanshan Defends Tongbei

Harbin Correspondence - After 3:00 PM on the 6th, the Self-Defense Army unit led by Yang Zibin engaged in a fierce battle with the Japanese Nakamura Brigade and the puppet Jilin army near Acheng. Four Japanese aircraft flew in at 4:00 PM to drop bombs. The battle is still ongoing. It is learned that the Self-Defense Army unit led by Yang Zibin consists of three regiments in total, including one cavalry regiment, one artillery regiment, and one infantry regiment. They first joined forces with Ma Xianzhang's army to attack Acheng on the morning of the 29th of last month, and once recovered it. However, on June 3rd, they retreated due to a counterattack by the Japanese Nakamura Brigade. On the night of the 4th, Ma Xianzhang's troops cut the telephone and telegraph lines between Fuyu and Shuangcheng, and there was news of an attack on Yushu. Yang Zibin's troops retreated along the eastern section of the Chinese Eastern Railway (CER) Harbin-Suifenhe line to Mulin Station, and incidentally attacked Maoershan Station, confiscating some firearms from the puppet Jilin army. Afterwards, they retreated into the mountains to reorganize and gather nearby Self-Defense Army units. They then advanced to Ercengjianzi on the morning of the 6th, using one regiment to flank Acheng and two regiments to attack from the front. One large unit of Japanese troops and approximately 2,000 puppet Jilin soldiers in Acheng came out to meet them outside the city at 3:00 PM. For operational convenience, the Japanese troops immediately set fire to the civilian houses outside the city, claiming it would reduce the Self-Defense Army's cover. As a result, many farmers lost their homes and had nowhere to settle, so they brought their old and young to Harbin to seek refuge. The number is extremely large. Eastbound passenger and freight trains on the CER have been suspended accordingly, and traffic on the Harbin-Suifenhe line has been completely cut off. The Russian director of the CER Railway Bureau specifically stated that he would not operate trains on the Harbin-Suifenhe line without adequate protection, in order to avoid endangering the lives of passengers. It is reported that Japanese troops are stationed in Mianpo, Wugimihe, and Hailin along the Harbin-Suifenhe line. Wugimi, Weishahe, and Hengdaohezi in the eastern section are guarded by the Self-Defense Army and National Salvation Army, who do not disturb local merchants at all, and merchants are able to conduct business peacefully. Approximately two brigades of Japanese troops are stationed on the Harbin-Suifenhe line, but they can do nothing about the Self-Defense Army. As the Self-Defense Army attacked Acheng, Xing Zhanqing also led more than 10,000 "Big Sword Society" members to Liaoshunzi (approximately 60 li from Harbin) east of Harbin to support Yang's army. The military situation on this front may become more intense. The military situation on the Hulan-Hailun route has come to an end. On the morning of the 3rd, the Japanese Hiraga Brigade, along with six aircraft, launched a fierce attack on Wu Songlin's brigade of the Heilongjiang army in Nihe. Wu's brigade was entirely cavalry, and the horses were bombed and scattered, leading to defeat. The artillery of Shi Lanbin's unit was weak and unable to resist the Japanese army's superior forces, so they also retreated. After the Japanese troops built a pontoon bridge and crossed the Nihe River, they arrived in Hailun at noon. Ma Zhanshan, who was in Tongbei, immediately gathered forces in that area and dug trenches between Beianzhen and Tongbei. At the same time, Heilongjiang troops from various places also concentrated in that direction. Infantry, cavalry, and the "Big Sword

Society" gathered together, numbering more than 10,000 people, and built solid trenches to prepare for a long-term defense. Cai Hongyou and Li Tiande's units, numbering approximately 3,000 people, recently moved from Wangkui and Qingcheng to the Fifth Station south of Wangkui, intending to launch a flanking attack and raid the Japanese base in Suihua. The Japanese army has dug trenches in that area for defense and has opened airfields in Hulan and Suihua. Airplanes are sent to Wangkui and Tongbei daily for reconnaissance. According to those who have returned, there are many righteous army infantrymen in the Baiquan area, and they are currently being transported to Tongbei. Li Haiqing's army, which is cooperating with Ma Zhanshan's army, was forced to retreat by the Japanese army on the 3rd.

to Anda, taking advantage of the Japanese army's unpreparedness in Hongjiadian south of Anda, surrounding and attacking fiercely, annihilating more than 200 enemies and capturing many military supplies. Japanese aircraft flew to bomb, and the Hiramatsu Regiment was dispatched early on the 4th to rescue the remnants, taking the opportunity to occupy Anda County. Li's army then retreated to Huojiaji, intending to move to Wangkui to approach Hailun and join forces with Ma Zhanshan's army. On the morning of the 5th, Japanese aircraft flew to Huojiaji to drop bombs. Li's army lay on the ground and used rifles to counterattack. They retreated leisurely on the afternoon of the 5th. On the afternoon of the 6th, it was reported that they had arrived north of Hailun. (6th)

He Zhuguo

Talks on Bitterly Defending Yuguan

Soldiers find unparalleled joy in killing foreign enemies

The Battle of Shanghai is an external illness, Yuguan is consumption.

Beiping Correspondence - He Zhuguo, the Ninth Brigade Commander stationed at Shanhaiguan, came to Beiping with the investigation team some days ago. The reporter visited him yesterday and recorded his conversation as follows: (Reporter asked) What attitude should your brigade take in defending Shanhaiguan in the future? (He replied) It is a soldier's duty to defend the country. Moreover, fighting against foreign countries is a once-in-a-lifetime opportunity for a true soldier. They should find unparalleled joy in killing the enemy. The Japanese Tianjin Garrison Army is located in the south of my brigade's defense, the South Sea and the west road, Taihuangdao, and the Japanese Kwantung Army is located outside the Guan. This is what is called being attacked from all sides. In my personal opinion, when the situation in Yuguan became tense after the 15th of last month, I made all preparations. After thinking it over, I should obey two principles: (1) Soldiers obey the orders of the highest commander, and (2) a few people consider the safety of the majority. If a war breaks out, North China will be shaken. If preparations are not complete, the impact will be even greater. Moreover, since I have not received orders from above, I can only endure humiliation and bear the heavy burden. However, I must defend every inch of the country's territory to the death and dare not fail to fulfill my mission. (Asked) What are the brigade commander's thoughts on the 19th Route Army? (Answer) The 19th Route Army fought bravely against the Japanese and promoted the spirit of the nation. I admire them immeasurably. However, the two months of fighting by the 19th Route Army was like suffering from an external illness. Once the acute phase passes, the illness will disappear. My brigade has been bitterly defending Shanhaiguan for nine months, and it is like suffering from consumption. We are still struggling and suffering. (Asked) The brigade commander's loyalty and courage in defending Yuguan are admirable. Who does the brigade commander intend to compare himself to in ancient times to repay the country? (Answer) Since ancient times, generals who have led troops to defend the border have had only two options: peace and war. The situation I am in is neither war nor peace. There has never been such a difficult situation since ancient times. If the arrangements are not careful, the Japanese army may be able to use it as an excuse. Wouldn't it be like a free city outside Shanghai and another free pass in the north? Now I can only defend the territory and repay the country. Who am I to compare myself to famous generals of ancient times? (Asked) The brigade commander came to Beiping with the investigation team. Did you hear any thoughts on the Manchurian state from Lord Lytton? (Answer) Although I did not hear it from Lord Lytton's mouth, the people around the investigation team all felt that "when they first arrived in Manchuria, they thought the Manchurian state had a foundation. When they arrived in Harbin and heard the sound of cannons and the activities of the Volunteer Army, they realized that the Manchurian state was very dangerous and that the foundation of its construction was only on the railway." He also said that I only know

to obey orders to defend the country's territory, and do everything in practice, without relying on propaganda. Propaganda must focus on reality. Excessive propaganda may inadvertently lead to disputes. He also said that although I came to Beiping to ask for instructions, the Yuguan army has a chief of staff as my proxy, and we communicate by telephone every day. The situation is currently very good, and I will return to defense the day after tomorrow. (10th)

League of Nations Investigation Team

A Day's Record of Visiting Qingdao

Qingdao Correspondence - Lord Lytton, Chairman of the League of Nations Investigation Team, and Mr. Schnee, the German representative, Mr. Codi, the Italian representative, and representatives from China and Japan, as well as many attendants, arrived in Qingdao from Jinan at 9:15 PM tonight (the 9th). The situation is recorded as follows:

Preparations in Advance - Mayor Shen Honglie ordered the Marine Corps and the Public Security Bureau to inform their subordinates that they must provide strict protection when the investigation team arrives in Qingdao. Therefore, the Railway Bureau police were responsible for guarding the inside of the station, and the Public Security Bureau secretly deployed posts outside the station and in the city. The area of vigilance was also stipulated. The area east of Chengbao and west of Songgezhuang was guarded by the Marine Corps stationed in the area. Songgezhuang to Cangkou was under the jurisdiction of the Sixth Branch of the Public Security Bureau, Cangkou to Sifen was under the jurisdiction of the Fifth Branch, Sifen to Dagang was under the jurisdiction of the Third and Fourth Branches, Dagang to the north end of Zhongshan Road was under the jurisdiction of the Second and Third Branches, and the north end of Zhongshan Road to the station, passing Guangxi, Jiangsu, and Yishui Roads, was under the jurisdiction of the First Branch. The area along the road outside the station was handled by the Second Security Team in conjunction with the First Branch, and the mayor's residence was guarded by the First Security Team.

Arrival in Qingdao - Around 7:00 PM, the Qingdao station inside and outside was guarded by the Railway Police and the Public Security Bureau Police Security Team. Around 8:00 PM, representatives from all walks of life who came to welcome them arrived at the station one after another, totaling approximately 200 people. Shen Honglie and important figures from the navy also

Page 8

arrived at the station. At 8:30 PM, the pilot car arrived first. At 9:15 PM, the special train entered the station. The train had a total of twelve cars, all of which were specially prepared coaches on the Beining Railway. After Lord Lytton and others got off the train, they briefly exchanged greetings with Mayor Shen and consuls from various countries. Then, they tipped their hats to the representatives from all walks of life, and then walked out of the station to take the cars prepared by the city government to the traveling headquarters. Lord Lytton and the German and Italian representatives all stayed at the Yingbin Hotel (i.e., the mayor's residence), while Representative Gu and other attendants stayed at the Wanguo Sanatorium. The Japanese representative, Yoshida, and his attendants stayed at the Grand Hotel.

Tour Itinerary - The team will stay in Qingdao for one day. Before 9:00 AM on the 10th, they will meet with representatives from all walks of life. At 9:00 AM, they will visit Mayor Shen at the city government. Then, they will go to Huiquan Bathing Beach, First Park, Battery, and other places for sightseeing. At 12:00 PM, they will return to the mayor's residence for lunch. After a short rest, they will visit the scenic Laoshan. They will have refreshments at Liushutai and return to Qingdao that evening. At 9:00 PM, they will take the original train west to Jinan and then to Taian. On the 11th, they will visit Mount Tai, and on the 12th, they will return to Beiping. (June 10th)

Passing Through Jinan to Visit Mount Tai

Report Writing Location to be Determined in Qingdao

Lytton Seems to Tacitly Accept the Japanese Claim

Jinan Correspondence - The Japanese had made thorough preparations in advance for Lord Lytton and others to come to Qingdao this time. A Japanese oil merchant in Qingdao named Minemura has an excellent house that had already been drawn up in advance, renovated and brand new. Therefore, as soon as the investigation team arrived in Qingdao, the Japanese representative, Yoshida, led Lord Lytton and others to inspect the house, showed them the drawings, and proposed that if the investigation team wrote the report in Qingdao, then

the house would be their residence. Lord Lytton and others seemed to agree to this proposal. If this becomes a reality, then the investigation team will be completely surrounded by the Japanese in the future. Because Lord Lytton and his party had to rush back to Beiping before noon on the 12th and planned to take time out of their busy schedule to visit Mount Tai, they only stayed in Qingdao for one day and left Qingxi at 6:20 PM on the 10th. Peng Dongyuan, a member of the Jiaoji Railway Committee, took a pilot car in advance. Lord Lytton and others are scheduled to arrive in Jinan at 3:30 AM on the 11th, and then transfer to the Tianjin-Pukou Railway. After the locomotive has been loaded with coal and water, it will depart for Taian at 4:00 AM. After arriving in Taian at 7:00 AM, they will climb the mountain to visit scenic spots. They will leave Taian at 5:00 PM and return north, passing through Jinan at 8:00 PM on the evening of the 12th

They are scheduled to arrive in Beiping before noon. A telegram was sent in advance to request the Jinan authorities not to welcome them at the station and not to prepare a military band. Jinan has had continuous hot weather in recent days. At 12:00 midnight on the 10th, there was a sudden thunderstorm, and the streets turned into rivers, one, two, three, or four feet deep. Zhang Honglie, the representative of Han Fuju, Wen Chenglie, the mayor of Jinan, Wang Kairu, the director of the Public Security Bureau, and others braved the rain to arrive at the Jiaoji Station to welcome Lord Lytton and others at 3:00 AM on the 11th. Lord Lytton's special train arrived at the Jinan Station at 4:15 AM due to delays en route. By then, the rain had stopped and the sky had cleared, and the golden rooster crowed. At 4:55 AM, they left Jinan and departed for Taian. Zhang Honglie traveled south with the train to host them. It is reported that the team is still scheduled to leave Taibei at 5:00 PM. (11th)

Japanese Young Officer Corps

Plotting to Assassinate Saitō Again

Cut Throat Letter Sent by Mail

Government and Councilors in Panic

Tokyo Mancho Newspaper reported that the severity of the guard inside and outside the Diet since the Diet opened has been unprecedented. Unexpectedly, at 10:00 AM on the second day, a confidential letter was suddenly sent by post to influential members of the House of Peers. The letter contained a "Cut Throat Letter to assassinate Prime Minister Saitō, Internal Minister Makino, and Wakatsuki, the President of the Minseitō," signed by the Young Officer Blood Alliance. When someone finished reading it at the time, he immediately notified all parties, and the government authorities and members of the House of Peers and the House of Representatives were greatly panicked. At the same time, the government, based on this letter, secretly ordered a thorough investigation and mutually discussed prudent preventive measures.

Compilation and Translation of Japanese Telegrams

Unprecedented News Occurs in the Japanese Judicial World - Tokyo Kokumin Newspaper reported that the Tokyo High Court recently discovered unprecedented news, that is, the same judge issued completely opposite verdicts on the same case on the same day. One verdict stated that the plaintiff won the case, and the other stated that the plaintiff lost the case, confusing both parties as to what to do.

The case was the bankruptcy of Ishii Sadashichi, who borrowed five koku of rice.

The main text and reasons for the verdict, as well as the legal interpretations, were absolutely contradictory. The parties on both sides received this document on the same day, and were all

surprised and at a loss as to what to do. One of the main texts was to cancel the original judgment and send it back to the Tokyo District Court for retrial. The other main text was to reject and not accept the case, that is, the former recognized that the original judgment was inappropriate and belonged to the winner, while the latter recognized that the original trial was proper and became a loser. However, the main text was like this, and the reasons stated in it were also greatly contradictory. (According to the darkness of the Japanese judicial world, how can there be organization?)

Japanese Immigration to Manchuria May Reach 1.5 Million People - Tokyo Kokumin Newspaper reported that the number of Japanese in Harbin suddenly increased by 1,500 in the past two months. Other inspection groups from the mainland, Korea, and South Manchuria continued to arrive in Harbin in an endless stream. All hotels were overcrowded. It is reported that the number of Japanese people who will immigrate to Manchuria in the future is estimated to be around 1.5 million. Therefore, the population of various cities and municipalities in Manchuria is gradually increasing sharply.

Japanese Secretly Supply the Righteous Army with Military Equipment - Tokyo Hochi Newspaper reported that four people, including Takasugi Shinichi, a citizen of Onomichi, secretly supplied the enemy (referring to our country) with military equipment and ammunition during the Sino-Japanese Incident. Kasaara Gunjirō, etc. of Omachi 2-chome, Fukushima City, dispatched them to Osaka on April 26 to secretly transport 100 Belgian-made twelve-shot pistols and 1,000 bullets packed in four wooden boxes, and sent them from the Abu County, Yamaguchi Prefecture Ogi Station. On May 30, Kasahara shipped the car and transported it to the steamship staying in Shinkawako, Ogi Town. Just as he was carrying it, he was suddenly discovered by the Ogi police officer, who brought him to the police station along with the witness. After a thorough investigation, it was revealed that there were accomplices in each port in Osaka and Moji. The authorities attached great importance to this traitorous act.

Europe and the United States Will Continue to Send Personnel to Investigate Manchuria - Tokyo Jiji Shinpo reported from Harbin that, according to information from foreign countries, after the League of Nations Lytton and other investigation committee reports, a meeting will be held to discuss the Manchurian issue and decide to further clarify the actual situation in Manchuria. Several military experts will be dispatched.

Entering Manchuria from Siberia and re-investigating the situation.

Chiang and He Confer on Bandit Suppression

Climbing Mount Lu Together on the 9th

Nanchang Correspondence - After Chiang Kai-shek sent a telegram to He Yingqin, Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in the Border Areas of Jiangxi, Guangdong, and Fujian, and Xiong Shihui, Chairman of the Jiangxi Provincial Government, from Nanjing on the 7th, they took a special train on the Nanchang-Jiujiang Road at 7:00 AM on the 8th to Jiujiang to welcome them. According to the telegrams received by the Headquarters and the Provincial Government, Chiang arrived in Jiujiang by ship at 6:00 AM on the 9th. When the ship docked, He and Xiong boarded the ship to pay their respects. After a short rest, Chiang and He Xiong disembarked one after another and went straight to Mount Lu. It is reported that Chiang believes that the Red Peril in the East China Sea is now the most severe in Hubei, while Jiangxi Province is the most extensive bandit area, and Jiangxi Province is also the center of the anti-communist military affairs of the seven southeastern provinces. In addition, since Chen Jitang withdrew a part of the Guangdong army that came to Jiangxi and Fujian to assist in bandit suppression, the original three-province bandit suppression plan must be re-planned. Therefore, Chiang went to Mount Lu with He and Xiong for a short stay in order to solve the above problems. It is reported that He also brought the three-province bandit suppression plan and report book when he went to Jiujiang to present to Chiang for approval. Chiang must decide on the bandit suppression plans for Jiangxi and other provinces in Mount Lu before going to Wuhan. Therefore, the date of departure for Jiujiang is still unknown. (10th)

Western Anhui

Red Bandits Return to Southern Henan

The Fourth Division Concentrates on Zhengyang

The Ninth Division Will be Stationed in Bengbu

Bengbu Correspondence - Because the official army launched a large-scale campaign to suppress them, the old nest of the Red Bandits in western Anhui led by Kuang Jixun was attacked. They have led most of the ferocious bandits to the area of Shangcheng, Guangshan, and Huangchuan in southern Henan. Liu Zhi, the Pacification Director of Kaifeng, also sent Chen Jicheng, Li Sisuo, and other troops to attack Guanghuang. Zhang Fang, the commander-in-chief of the 20th Route Army, also ordered his troops to cooperate with the militia to encircle and suppress the bandits in Shangcheng. The Air Force stationed in Bengbu sent planes carrying bombs to the Huang area for reconnaissance and bombing for days. The bandit forces are declining day by day, and it is hoped that they will be cleared up soon. As for the Red Bandits in Huoqiu, a part of them still remains and has seized wheat in order

to transport it to the bandit area. The bandits have deployed defenses in the Xihu area west of Huoqiu and guard Yulindian. This group is mostly local bandits who have been newly incorporated into the Red Army, known as the Red Guards, and are not purely communists, so they do not have any real strength. The Huoqiu, Yingshang, Zhengyang area militia has a crowd of four or five thousand people. After the fall of Zhengyang, they launched attacks on the bandits repeatedly. From last month to the present, they have fought fiercely with the bandits five times, but they have been unable to eliminate the bandits due to lack of ammunition and uncoordinated command. At present, defenses are deployed above the Huai River, in the Linhuaigang, Tianjiagang, Xindianbu, Zhangtaizi, and Jiangtaizi areas. People from Yingshang said that if there were strong troops to suppress them, the bandits would be easily defeated. It is also very strange that the Song Shike Brigade stationed in Zhengyang did not dare to cross the Lei Pond. The representatives of the five counties of Huoqiu, Fuyang, Yingshang, Shou County, and Fengtai asked for assistance in Beijing, saying that the militia of each county lacked ammunition and their strength was quite insufficient. They requested the Military Affairs Commission to allocate ammunition for the militia for bandit suppression and self-defense. The Military Affairs Commission approved and ordered Xu Tingyao, the commander of the Fourth Division, to allocate 100,000 rounds for the five counties to receive. Huofu Yinghou Feng and five counties have sent representatives to Bengbu to receive and apply for use. The Fourth Division recently received an order from the Military Affairs Commission to go to Zhengyang to search and suppress the Red Bandits and protect farmers in harvesting wheat. Xu Tingyao decided to send six infantry regiments to concentrate on Zhengyang and advance towards Huoqiu. Xu will also go to Zhengyang to command the troops to suppress the bandits. The

The Independent Brigade of the division, led by Guan Linzheng, departed by boat from Bengbu to the west on the afternoon of the 10th. The First Supplementary Regiment stationed in Huaiyuan departed on the morning of the 11th and was stationed in Shou County. The situation in Shoucheng has eased. The 11th Brigade, led by Wang Wanling, is scheduled to depart from Bengbu and head west on the 12th. The 12th Brigade and the officers and soldiers directly under the师司令部各处官兵直属部队各处官兵直属部队 each division headquarters are scheduled to depart Zhengyang on the 13th. The division headquarters will be established there. The division recently received an order to return to the command of Wang Jun, the commander of the Third Army stationed in Hefei. Wang is scheduled to convene a bandit suppression meeting within the day to determine the bandit suppression plan and combat strategy in order to achieve effective command. Xu Tingyao will send personnel to Hefei to participate in the meeting. As the Fourth Division set off to suppress the bandits, the defense of Bengbu will be taken over by Li Yiannian's Ninth Division under the command of Jiang Dingwen, commander of the Second Army. The Bandit World of Southern Anhui

Merchant Ships Robbed Again and Again

Wuyuan Soldiers and Bandits Fight Fiercely

Wuhu Correspondence - Small steamers operating between Beijing, the provincial capital Wuhu, and various inland river areas

have been repeatedly robbed midway by bandits. Some days ago, the Wuan merchant ship of the Datong class and the Wuning small steamer of the Jingwu class were robbed one after another, and people were brutally killed. The two cases have no clues. Yesterday, the Kuailong merchant ship of the Yilong Company, which sailed from Wuwu County to Wuhu, carrying more than 200 passengers, suddenly found more than 20 bandits on the ship, each with a pistol, forcing the ship to stop and looting. The passengers' clothes were mostly stripped, with losses of more than 5,000 yuan. After the ship arrived in Wuhu, the robbed passengers believed that the ship seemed to have noticed the presence of bandits beforehand and had moved and hid the tickets and other items, but did not inform the public in order to prepare for it. Therefore, they intend to negotiate with the ship company to investigate.

The Red Bandits of Anhui Province have been accumulating and maintaining themselves until now and have become a major problem. It is heard that the number of bandits and guns in the Liu'an area of western Anhui has reached more than 40,000, which is almost equal to the bandit situation in Fujian and Jiangxi. In southern Anhui, the Huizhou area, there are also often bandits appearing. The business community here recently received a telegram from Wuyuan, saying that County Mayor Ke of the county fought fiercely with the bandits yesterday. Relying on the bravery of the police, many bandits were killed and 11 staff members of the bandit party were captured. The chase is still underway. It can be known that the bandit situation is all over the Anhui territory. (10th)

Qiongyai

War Imminent

Chen Jitang Orders Army and Air Force to Assemble in Leizhou

Chen Ce Sends Navy to Raid Beihai

Guangzhou Correspondence: A month has passed since the Guangdong naval and air forces were reorganized and placed under new command, sparking a disturbance. Numerous attempts at mediation have failed, as both sides have become so polarized that mediation is impossible. The delay in resolving the issue with force is due to the lack of opportune timing. Investigations reveal that the province has completed its military preparations, and the troops dispatched to attack Hainan have arrived in Leizhou in succession, creating a confrontational situation with Hainan. The Hainan navy has consistently opposed the provincial authorities, as evidenced by their slogans in a Hainan newspaper, which vehemently criticized Chen Jitang. This demonstrates their resolute determination. Since concentrating in Hainan, the navy has withheld tax revenues from Hainan's thirteen counties. On the 2nd and 3rd of this month, the navy sent a battalion of marines under Chen Ji, aboard the warship "Flying Eagle," to Lianzhou. Landing at Beihai, they seized all taxes and ordered Beihai merchants to raise 200,000 yuan for military expenses within three days. Chen Jitang, fearing that the marines would occupy Qinlian, has ordered Chen Hanguang's guard brigade stationed in Gaozhou to advance with all speed. The vanguard of Chen's brigade arrived in Leizhou on the 2nd, while the brigade headquarters and the regiment led by Liang Guowu have reached Xuwen, deploying along the Leizhou coast. The Third Independent Regiment, led by Zhang Wentao, arrived on the 4th, and the Fourth Independent Regiment, led by Liu Qishi, will soon depart from Gaozhou southward. The provincial government is mobilizing approximately a brigade and three regiments, totaling over 20,000 troops, for the attack on Hainan. However, Xuwen in Leizhou is about 200 nautical miles from Hainan's port, separated by the Qiongzhou Strait, making a swift crossing difficult. The fleet only possesses a couple of warships, such as the "Haihu," which is insufficient. Therefore, thorough preparations are necessary for the attack. To compensate for the lack of naval vessels, Chen Jitang has procured a large quantity of fir to build rafts for transporting troops across the sea to land. He has also decided to deploy the air force to control the Hainan navy's activities, given their superior combat strength. Chen has ordered Huang Guangrui, the air force commander, to recall a portion of the Fifth Air Force squadron from Shantou and reallocate five new fighter planes from the province, bringing the total to eleven. They are to be deployed to Leizhou, enabling a simultaneous land and air attack. According to a telegram from the Southern District Pacification Headquarters, the Leizhou airfield was completed on the 4th of this month, and the planes for the Hainan campaign will soon be stationed there awaiting orders. On the land front, Chen Jitang has mobilized a division of the Second Army to Gaozhou as a backup, to bolster his forces. Fearing that Hainan's navy might intercept sea transports along the coast, the supplies are being transported by land. Supply depots have been established, with the main depot in Zhaoqing and branch depots in Yangjiang, Maoming, Leicheng, and Xuwen. Military supplies and rations are constantly being transported. On the evening of the 4th, four large cannons and a large quantity of military supplies and ammunition were transported from headquarters to the front for the attack on Hainan. It seems that war on Hainan is imminent. (June 8)

Local Correspondence

Suzhou

Public Security Bureau Arrests a Large Number of Communists: The Public Security Bureau, acting on orders to investigate suspected Communists, dispatched a large number of inspectors, along with personnel from various sub-bureaus and stations, to conduct searches at designated addresses. They arrested carpenter Wang A'bao in the First Sub-Bureau's jurisdiction; Jiang Tieru, Yue Zongfei, and Chen Nannian in the Second Sub-Bureau's jurisdiction; eight Hongsheng Match Factory workers, including Zhang Yonglian, Liu Qiqing, Lao Lianfu, Gao Shunfu, Gao A'fa, Han Renfang, Yang Gongming, and Gu Gengquan, in the Third Sub-Bureau's jurisdiction; Wang Xiao'a'san, a worker from the Sulun Factory; and Lu Mo and Bu Shifan, two teachers from Bantang Primary School. All were taken to the main bureau and then escorted to the Capital Garrison Headquarters for processing.

Notorious Bandit Gu Jiwen and Accomplices Executed: Gu Jiwen, Shen Decai, Xue Song'a, and others, notorious bandits who robbed the 19th Route Army's transportation boat, murdered Deputy Director Wang of the army's transportation department, robbed the Susheng ferry, and plundered wealthy refugees in Wuxi, were captured. After being interrogated by the Songhu Anti-Bandit Command, they were sentenced to death. Yesterday (the 12th), they were escorted by ship to the scene of their crimes and executed by firing squad.

New Education Bureau Director to Take Office: The newly appointed Director of the Education Bureau, Peng Jiazhi, is scheduled to take office on the 15th of this month. He is currently investigating the bureau's financial deficits and seeking ways to raise funds.

Wuxi

Finance Department Enforces the "Yitu" System: During the early Guangxu period of the Qing dynasty, under the leadership of Pei Dazhong, the magistrate of Wuxi, the "Yitu" system was implemented in Wuxi. Land taxes were assigned to a "Jia Zhu" (head of the "Jia"), who was responsible for collecting and remitting the full amount. Over the decades, many "Jia Zhu" were bankrupted or fled due to covering the tax shortfalls. As a result, people were reluctant to take on the role. Recently, the Jiangsu Finance Department, recognizing the increasing difficulty in collecting outstanding land taxes, has formulated rules to rigorously implement the "Yitu" system in all counties. Every village will nominate a wealthy individual to serve as "Jia Zhu" on a rotating annual basis, responsible for collecting the full amount of land taxes. Wuxi and Wujin counties will be the first to implement this system, starting with the winter grain tax this year. The county government has been ordered to comply.

Changzhou

Wounded Soldier Chen Xiaocheng, Who Caused Trouble, Arrested: The joint police and militia inspection office of Wuyi Province arrested Chen Xiaocheng, a discharged soldier who had committed multiple crimes. Investigations revealed that he had forced the Dexing Pawnshop in Xicang Bridge to lend him money using a steel watch as collateral, leading to a conflict with the Western Business Corps. He had also seized firearms from the Public Security Bureau's wooden-shell squad, injured squad members, and robbed the Yong'an Tea House of twenty silver dollars. He was identified by the victims and sent to the county for trial on the evening of the 11th.

Zhenjiang

Illegal Inspection Office Robs Opium: Numerous opium robberies have occurred along the river in the provincial capital, with five or six incidents in recent days. It is rumored that various agencies are investigating the matter, but none have claimed responsibility. Recently, Wang Hongxun set up an illegal inspection office in Daguanlou and seized opium on two occasions. After being reported to the court, he was summoned by the prosecutor's office, but Wang refused to appear. It is said that the prosecutor's office has issued another summons with a warrant for arrest.

Ministry Orders Abolition of Special Business Tax: The Ministry of Finance of the Executive Yuan has ordered the Jiangsu Provincial Government to abolish the proposed special business tax. It is said that the provincial government claims that only one million yuan is available for provincial expenses this year, which is far from sufficient. Therefore, the special business tax is deemed necessary. The Director of the Finance Department recently met with representatives from Suzhou and Wuxi chambers of commerce, expressing the provincial government's plight and seeking understanding. However, various parties expressed strong opposition and refused to accept the tax. It is said that the majority of cotton and wood subject to the special tax are foreign goods, and collecting the tax may violate the original intent of tariff reduction and tax increases. The Finance Department is reconsidering the proposal and considering replacing the business tax with a business license tax. The tax rate will be divided into three classes and nine grades, with a maximum monthly tax of fifty yuan and a minimum monthly tax of five jiao for businesses with capital under 100,000 yuan. Businesses with capital above 100,000 yuan will be subject to separate regulations. Director Shu of the Finance Department is scheduled to invite executive committee members of the Provincial Federation of Commerce on the 13th to discuss provincial finance and tax issues. According to the executive committee members, the business tax can be assisted within their capacity, based on the principle of cooperation between officials and citizens. However, they will not intervene in the special business tax or the business license tax.

Yangzhou

Refused Bandits at the Door, Died by Bullet: When bandits came to the residence of She Wenxun in Yang'er Township, the eighth district of the county, he closed the door to resist. Unable to enter, the bandits fired randomly. A bullet penetrated the wall and entered She's mouth, causing him to collapse. After learning of the incident from nearby villages, they sounded the alarm, causing the bandits to flee. However, She lost too much blood and died on the way to the city for treatment. It is reported that the incident has been reported to the authorities for redress.

Gaoyou

Province Orders Joint Survey of Dike Construction by Two Counties: Yan Zuobin of Baoying, who was previously responsible for constructing the southern dike of Baoying, changed the route without authorization and forcibly excavated farmland in Gaoyou, illegally arresting farmers' representatives such as Shen Furong. Farmers led by Liu Tianguan have filed a complaint with the provincial government. It is reported that the Civil Affairs Department has instructed the Gaoyou and Baoying county governments to conduct a joint survey and submit a factual report for review. The Gaoyou county government has dispatched Deng Linzhu, the head of the First Section, to conduct the survey.

Jiaxing

Clues Found in Kidnapping Case in Xuejiagang: In Xuejiagang (only ten miles from the city) in Jiaxing County, the homes of Feng Jiande and Feng Zuoqing were robbed and Feng Wu, Feng Zuoqing's granddaughter-in-law, was kidnapped last month. After the incident, the Second District of the Water Police sent detectives to investigate and arrested Yang Wenbiao, a resident of Taiwan, near Sanjiaozhi, a location close to the home, for questioning. However, they released Yang because there was no evidence to link him to the crime, and Yang did not confess to colluding with the bandits. Recently, the district police arrested Pan A'san, a suspect in the case. The victim identified him as one of the robbers. After interrogation, Pan confessed to the robbery and claimed that the kidnapped woman was hidden in Yang Wenbiao's straw hut. As a result, Yang was arrested again and confronted with Pan. Pan told Yang to quickly hand over the kidnapped woman to avoid further suffering, but Yang denied it. Efforts are underway to find the woman so she can be rescued.

Hangzhou

Apprentice Embezzles Funds, Commits Suicide by Drowning: Wu Yongquan, a sixteen-year-old apprentice at the tea shop owned by Wang Ziqing in Shangqianbu, Hangzhou, diligently served and gained Wang's trust. He was entrusted with handling money. However, a gambler named Ye Jinbiao, taking advantage of his youth and naivety, lured him into gambling. Wu fell for the scheme and gradually embezzled over 300 yuan from the shop, losing it all. Filled with regret and fearing that Wang would discover his actions, he secretly went to the riverbank the night before and drowned himself. The next morning, his body was found floating in the water.

Wang immediately sent a letter to Wu's father, Ju Huan, to inform him of the situation. After learning the cause of death, he brought Ye Jinbiao to the local Public Security Bureau and notified the Hangzhou District Court to send someone to examine the body. Ye was arrested and detained by the court.

Military Vehicle Kills Elderly Man: A vehicle from the 106th Ordnance Depot of the Ministry of Military Administration struck and killed Yan Quanfu, a 73-year-old tailor, near the city station the other day. The depot has provided Yan's family with 100 yuan for funeral expenses and sent the driver, soldier Wang Zhen, to the Hangzhou District Court for questioning. Wang claimed that he was unable to brake in time. The court determined that the vehicle belonged to the Ministry of Military Administration, and the driver was a soldier, so the case did not fall under the court's jurisdiction. It was transferred to the Provincial Security Department for further investigation.

Xiaoshan

Cargo Ship Robbed at Xinjiangkou: A cargo ship sailing from Zhuji to Linpu on the night of the 8th near Xinjiangkou in Xiaoshan County was intercepted by over ten robbers wielding weapons and speaking with a Sheng dialect. They ordered the ship to stop and swarmed aboard, stealing fifteen bolts of foreign cloth and over forty silver dollars. They also stabbed Chen Xiaomao, a passenger from Dongyang, and fled. The shipowner, Yang Xiaoyuan, has reported the incident to the Xiaoshan and Zhuji county governments, requesting an investigation to ensure the safety of travelers.

Carelessness at Night Leads to Death of Two Children in Fire: A fire broke out at the Cai family residence in Caijia Village outside the South Gate of Xiaoshan County on the night of the 10th. A kerosene lamp overturned and ignited a mosquito net, causing a fire. Due to the late hour and strong winds, the fire spread quickly, destroying three buildings and killing two children, a cow, and two pigs. Over ten shih of wheat were also destroyed. The estimated loss is over 5,000 taels of silver.

Local News

Memorial Service in the Cold Wind and Bitter Rain

The Spirit of the Martyrs Will Never Die, Yet the Sun Loses Its Light

The Compatriots Sacrifice for the Country, Even Heaven Sheds Tears

The Shanghai Municipal Memorial Service for the Martyrs of the Songhu Resistance and the Compatriots Who Died in the Disaster was held at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday morning at ten o'clock amidst a cold wind and bitter rain. Thousands of people attended, filling almost every space in the venue. General Cai Tingkai, Mayor Wu Tiecheng, and others personally attended. In addition, Chief Officiant Wang Xiaolai, Central Representative Wang Luyi, and Supervisory Yuan Representative Gao Yihan also attended. The atmosphere was extremely desolate and solemn. All stores in the city flew their flags at half-mast to express their condolences. The details of yesterday's events are recorded below.

Arrangement of the Venue: The venue was the main auditorium inside the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. A sacrificial altar was set up in the center, with the chief officiant's seat in front, followed by the assisting officiant's seat, then the seats for representatives from Party, government, and military agencies, the press, and finally, the prompter's seat and conductor's seat. On both sides were the orchestra and alarm bell. Representatives from various sectors gathered inside the venue. The altar was covered with wreaths presented by Sun Ke, the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, Zhang Zhizhong, Wu Tiecheng, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and others, creating a splendid and solemn atmosphere. A horizontal banner above read: "Shanghai Municipal Memorial Service for the Martyrs of the Songhu Resistance and the Compatriots Who Died in the Disaster." The surroundings were filled with elegiac couplets, numbering no fewer than several hundred. Outside the venue, beneath the fluttering flags of the Party and the nation, a banner reading "Shanghai Municipal Memorial Service for the Martyrs of the Songhu Resistance and the Compatriots Who Died in the Disaster" was prominently displayed. Inside the corridor, striking cloth paintings were hung. Red ink blended with raindrops, dripping down like rain or blood.

Guards at the Gate: Yesterday morning at nine o'clock, representatives from various sectors began arriving. The General Police Department dispatched a large contingent of Western and Chinese police officers and detectives to stand guard outside the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and at the Tianhou Palace Bridge, North Henan Road, and North Suzhou Road. They also prohibited vehicles from passing through the section from Shanxi Road Bridge to Henan Road Bridge. Those with suspicious behavior were searched. Inside the gate, boy scouts from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Post Office, and the Moore Memorial Church strictly guarded the entrance, checking identification badges and refusing entry to those without them.

Solemn Elegiac Couplets: There were many elegiac couplets displayed at the venue yesterday, too numerous to list in detail. Among them were those with solemn and tragic wording, such as Zhang Zhizhong's: "Recalling the corpses filling Yunzao, blood dyeing Jiangwan, we are saddened by the sight of the war zone, tears flow down our faces in shame for surviving. Looking afar at the rebels occupying the White Mountains, the enemy invading the Black Water, we grieve for the ruined homeland, we will not share the sky with this enemy." Li Liejun's: "We rely on brave troops to defeat strong enemies, do not report the agreement to the heroic souls." Yu Jishi's: "Blood battles and hand-to-hand combat, but to restore our homeland, they lightly gave up their precious heads. Swallowing our tears, we recall the devastation by the Party, how can we bear to go to the depths of the underworld with such deep hatred?" Sun Ke's: "Evil forces spread, seawater flies horizontally, a strange disaster strikes early in the morning. Seeing the deep wounds suffered by Liaoshen and Songhu, we know that Han traitors cannot coexist with the righteous. Upholding justice and protecting our golden territory, we bravely defend what is right. Tracing back to Suiyang and Wu Mu defending the nation, in the underworld, we can all share the same hatred." Lin Jin's: "Zhabei, Jiangwan, and Wusongzhen, all reduced to scorched earth, the cuckoo cries out the blood of the nation. Washington, Hague, and Locarno, just a few scraps of paper, the crowing of a wild rooster awakens the soul from its dream." The couplets written by various trade associations were also remarkable.

Representatives Arrive: Wang Xiaolai of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Zhang Yichen of the Municipal Federation of Citizens, and Cao Zhigong of the General Federation of Commerce were the first to arrive. They were followed by Wang Luyi of the Central Executive Committee, Gao Yihan of the National Government Supervisory Yuan, Wu Tiecheng of the Military Affairs Commission and the Municipal Government, Cai Tingkai, the commander of the 19th Army, Fan Qiwu, the director of the Rear Affairs Office, Zhu Feinan, the chief of staff of the Fifth Army, Jiang Bingheng of the Ministry of Military Administration, Ye Baoqi of the Naval Headquarters, Zhang Xiang and Wen Ti of the Garrison Headquarters, Ye Hongji of the Foreign Affairs Office, Pan Gongzhan of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Dai Hongji of the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, Liang Renjie of the Third Branch, Chen Jianru representing Sun Ke, Lin Kanghou of the Bankers Association, Xu Shiying and E Runzhi of the Xinwei Relief Association, Zhu Qinglan and Cha Liangzhao of the Local Autonomy Association, Shen Junru of the Lawyers Association, and representatives of the National Crisis Relief Association, totaling over two thousand people.

The Memorial Ceremony: At ten o'clock in the morning, the announcement was made that the ceremony would begin. The China Alarm Bell Association rang the alarm bell twenty-one times, its resounding sound deeply resonating with those present. The chief officiant and assistant officiant then took their seats. Everyone stood in silence and bowed three times to the flags of the Party and the nation and the portrait of Sun Yat-sen, the founding father of the nation, sang the Party anthem, and bowed three times to the martyrs of the Songhu Resistance and the compatriots who died in the disaster, and observed three minutes of silence to mourn the martyrs of the Songhu Resistance and the compatriots who died in the disaster. Chief Officiant Wang Xiaolai delivered a eulogy and presented a flower garden, Party, government, and military representatives offered sacrifices, elegiac music was played, General Cai Tingkai delivered a speech, more elegiac music was played, and slogans were shouted. The ceremony concluded at eleven fifteen.

Eulogy by the Chief Officiant: Chief Officiant Wang Xiaolai's eulogy roughly stated: "Today, in the cold wind and bitter rain, we hold this solemn and enthusiastic memorial service for the martyrs of the Songhu Resistance and the compatriots who died in the disaster. When we recall the tragedy of January 28th up to this day, now that the war is over and we hold this memorial service, what are our thoughts? Personally, I have nothing to say at this meeting. Moreover, life is a hundred years, and death is inevitable. However, like a family, parents, children, enjoying the happiness of family life, but the parents die, what do they die for? In other words, the martyrs and compatriots who died in the Songhu Resistance did not sacrifice for themselves, but for the survival of the Chinese nation. If we can think of it this way, those of us who are not yet dead should continue the martyrs' hot blood, take responsibility, and work hard. We also feel that during the Songhu Resistance, our innocent people and great buildings in the Zhabei area were sacrificed and destroyed by enemy planes, bombs, and artillery shells in vain. Now, Wusong and Jiangwan have become wastelands. Therefore, on the one hand, we must remember the pain of the martyrs and innocent people, and adhere to the idiom "Never forget this day" and "Swear to avenge the national humiliation". On the other hand, we must unite to abolish the civil war, in order to be worthy of the martyrs and compatriots who died today. This is also the responsibility of those of us who survive."

General Cai Tingkai (center) Enters the Venue in the Rain (Photo Courtesy of Mr. Jiang Bingnan)

General Cai Tingkai's Speech: "Today, all sectors of Shanghai hold this memorial service for the martyrs of the Songhu Resistance and the compatriots who died in the disaster. I have come to participate, and I feel that this is the most tragic event. If the invaders are not expelled and the national crisis is not over, there is nothing more I can say. I only hope that we will unite to resist foreign aggression. The significance of today's meeting is extremely great, and it is not merely holding a memorial service and then finishing. The national crisis is pressing. Unless all compatriots unite to devise a plan to deal with it and fight to the end, we will not live up to the meaning of today's memorial service.

We hope to implement the anti-Japanese policy in the future, and we hope that all compatriots will work hard to move forward." His words were extremely painful, and all who heard them were moved.

General Cai Tingkai and Mr. Wang Xiaolai (Xu Tianzhang Photo) Delivering Speeches at the Meeting

Sacrificial Oration by the Ministry of Military Administration: On June 10, the Minister of Military Administration He Yingqin, Political Vice Minister Chen Yi, and Permanent Vice Minister Cao Haosen, offer this bouquet of fresh flowers to the spirits of the martyrs of the Songhu Resistance and the compatriots who died in the disaster, saying: Alas, Heaven is clouded, and we suffer this great calamity. The monkeys and cranes call out for souls, the dark earth turns to blood. Recalling the past, the conflict arose with our Eastern neighbor. With greedy eyes, they sought to swallow us. In an instant, they were like mad dogs, repeatedly displaying their ferocity, drooling over this piece of flesh. The banks of the Songjiang River became a war zone, and where the vicious ones went, the villages became ruins. Alas, my compatriots, rising up in anger, why live a life of ignominy, we would rather die. Seven feet tall, we received it from Heaven. We would rather be broken jade than whole tiles. The magnificent spirit fills the world, Confucius spoke of achieving benevolence, Mencius spoke of taking righteousness. Men serve the nation, deterring those vile barbarians. Once they die for righteousness, a hundred days of grief. Alas, we cry out to Heaven, the turbulent streams sob. Grieving for the past and mourning for the present, we are overwhelmed with sorrow.

Who does not die, but death is as heavy as Mount Tai. With lofty brows and outstanding features, their hearts and souls are fragrant. Departed compatriots, the national humiliation has not been avenged, let us learn from the predecessors, those who survive have a responsibility. This bouquet of fresh flowers is respectfully offered before your spirits. May you, in the underworld, know of this sincerity and good intentions. Accept this offering!

Sacrificial Oration by the Municipal Government: On June 12, of the 21st year of the Republic of China, Wu Tiecheng, the mayor of Shanghai, leading all colleagues of the Municipal Government, offer incense, flowers, wine, and libations to the spirits of the martyrs of the Songhu Resistance and the compatriots who died in the disaster, saying: Alas, bones cover the fields, blood fills the ditches, the squares are rubble, the dry trees are stumps. Who can read the text of an ancient battlefield without their tears wetting their sleeves? Alas, lamenting the decline of the nation, sighing at the perilous state of the country, politics are not cultivated, disasters encroach, and the whole country is apathetic as before. When people insult themselves, others will insult them. Although the neighboring countries are tyrannical, but our being looked down upon has a long history. Otherwise, how would the words "occupy Zhabei in four hours" dare to be spoken so freely? If not for the 45 days of resistance, how would we wash away the nation's shame and the nation's humiliation? Today, we can make the strong invaders tremble, and the world pay attention, thanks to the loyal and struggling generals and soldiers, and the compatriots who disregarded sacrifice. Alas, the dead are gone, the responsibilities of the living have become even greater. Can they maintain this glory and carry it forward, or will they lose it and be laughed at by the world? Alas, will we, descendants of the divine, bring ourselves to destruction? Why not change course, wash away the long-standing habits of decline, and strive for survival? Then the meaning of this war is even greater, and the value of the sacrifice is even more significant, and the eyes of the dead can be closed in peace. Otherwise, we are all sinners against the martyred soldiers, this glorious history will also fall to the ground, and the disaster of national subjugation and racial extinction is imminent. Shouldn't we be afraid? Wu Tiecheng and others are responsible for protecting the territory and securing the people, but cannot pacify the region, and cannot prevent disasters. Witnessing the intensity of the war, the brutality of the burning and killing, grieving for our soldiers and civilians, either filling the ditches or turning into insects, we cannot rescue them, and we cannot offer assistance. Our hearts are broken, we wipe our tears and sigh, we are distressed for months. Alas, swords and sabers move automatically, knowing that the spirits have never departed, banners still exist, the gods are still there. Therefore, we write the following: The fierce invaders are as violent as wolves and tigers, they treat us like fish to be slaughtered, alas, the people drink bullets and face the axe, great are our national troops, loyal and brave, death is as heavy as Mount Tai, their names will last forever, with grief and anger, we resist the foreign aggressors, alas, accept this offering.

Sacrificial Oration by the Municipal Party Headquarters: The Municipal Party Headquarters offers, with utmost sincerity, sacrifices to the spirits of the martyrs of the Songhu Resistance, saying:

Alas, the strong invaders press the border, they encroach upon us like silkworms and swallow us like whales. Having already seized our Eastern Province, they now eye our Shanghai. Malevolent energy fills the air, and righteousness fades away. Although we have a duty to defend our territory, who is there to protect the nation? It is our soldiers, brave and loyal, who vow to wield their weapons and sweep away the flames of the enemy. They pledge their hot blood to revitalize our undying national spirit. They would rather be smashed to pieces than surrender an inch of territory to the enemy. Therefore, they were able to awe all nations and move all three armies. Charging forward with bows and arrows, seizing flags and leading the charge, they decided ten times and won ten times, fought a hundred battles and won a hundred battles. For the sake of national freedom, for the sake of the survival of the nation, they treated danger as if it were flat ground, and regarded death as if it were life. Alas, martyrs, Mount Tai is heavy, a feather is light. They killed the enemy, defended the country, and saved the people. Although those who achieve benevolence may not necessarily succeed, those who succeed must first achieve benevolence. To kill the enemy and achieve the desired result, and to continue their work and fulfill their ambitions, is up to us, the survivors. Special Martial Law Yesterday Morning

A Memorial Service Also Held at the Public Sports Ground

More Than 500 People Dispersed by Police

Many Arrested, Briefly Admonished and Released

The Shanghai Citizens' United Association Against the Armistice Agreement and in Support of the Northeast Volunteers held a memorial meeting for the martyrs who died resisting Japan in Northeast China and Shanghai at the West Gate Public Sports Ground at 10:00 AM yesterday. The Municipal Public Security Bureau, fearing that thugs would infiltrate and take the opportunity to cause trouble, ordered the event prohibited and declared special martial law. Yesterday morning around 9:00 AM, representatives from various groups continuously arrived at the Public Sports Ground, preparing to hold the meeting when they were dispersed by the police. The situation was chaotic for a time, fortunately without any incident. Details of various aspects are recorded below:

Special Martial Law: The Municipal Public Security Bureau yesterday ordered police officers from each district police station to be fully armed and deployed for defense. Double sentries were stationed at all key points. The area around the West Gate Public Sports Ground was heavily guarded by police detachments, intensifying inspection of pedestrians. Patrol cars shuttled around the area. The iron gates at the borders of the French Concession were locked down, leaving only Xiaodongmen and Sanyang open.

Boy Scouts Maintaining Order at the Venue (Photo by Xu Tianzhang)

Jingqiao, Zhengjia Muqiao, Xiaobeimen, Nanyangqiao, and Xieqiao several places, trams passed through, and more Chinese and Western detectives were dispatched to guard the borders. The Public Concession Police Department also intensified preparations in the western and eastern districts of Shanghai.

Gathering to Protest: Yesterday morning around 9:00 AM, several dozen people resembling workers and students near the West Gate Public Sports Ground held bamboo flags inscribed with "Workers' Delegation of the Commercial Press Participating in the Memorial Meeting." The Municipal Public Security Bureau's police detachment and officers from the Second District General Office were stopping them when six large trucks from the China Moving Company suddenly arrived, filled with participants, flower wreaths, elegiac couplets, and flags. At that time, the police officers advised them not to gather during martial law, but the participants insisted, shouting various slogans, distributing leaflets, and forcibly opening the sports ground gate, rushing in. The police officers' attempts to stop them were ineffective. More trucks arrived, filled with workers and students from the textile factories, joining the participation. The total number of men and women exceeded 500, and they announced the start of the meeting.

Dispersing the Crowd: The Municipal Public Security Bureau, considering that the meeting was disobedient to advice, had the police detachment disperse the crowd. At that time, the meeting was in the process of electing a chairman, and the order was disrupted. The crowd retreated in droves towards the West Gate and Xieqiao, leaving flower wreaths, leaflets, and flags scattered all over the ground, shouting slogans. The Public Security Bureau also detained many individuals resembling workers and students, sending them to the General Bureau for handling. At the time, the police officers were ordered to be unarmed and did not carry guns, so no unfortunate incidents occurred.

Many Arrested: Unable to enter and hold the meeting, the crowd still lingered in the rain at the sports ground gate. The Public Security Bureau dispatched more police detachments to suppress them, explaining to the crowd that they were ordered to prohibit it. A few people negotiated with the police, resulting in minor clashes, and nine people were arrested by the Second District Chief of Police: Yuan Langgen, Lan Shouren, Chen Hui, Chen Beihai, Luo Baomin, Hu Moqian, Wu Choufa, Luo Beiguang, Wang Xiaolong, and others. They were taken to the district and transferred to the Public Security Bureau. The rest dispersed. All flags, leaflets, and elegiac couplets were discarded on the ground. Also, at 11:00 AM, when the crowd dispersed and paraded to the Bund area in the First District, fourteen people were arrested by the police precinct in that section: Li Jijun, Lin Laobin, Lin Yishu, Liu Zhichao, Yang Liansheng, Wan Lie, Ying Huairen, Zhang

Group Photo After the Meeting of Military Commander Cai (Photo by Xu Tianzhang)

Yue, Sun Zhi, Zhang Jinyu, Zhou Biguang, Wang Yueke, Lu Duanqing, Xie Chaoqun, and others. They were taken to the First District and sent to the Third Section of the Municipal Public Security Bureau for investigation. It was heard that after being briefly admonished, they were immediately released.

Traffic Disrupted: After receiving the report, the French Concession Police Department closed the iron gates at Nanyangqiao and other places at 10:30 AM, disrupting traffic. As a result, trams on Routes 17 and 18 from the Great World to Xieqiao were temporarily suspended. They had not resumed service by nightfall. At the same time, tram service on Route 6 of the French Tramway Company from West Gate to Xieqiao and public buses of the China General Omnibus Company from West Gate to Xieqiao were also suspended for about an hour. Services only resumed after the crowd dispersed.

Peaceful Evening: After the incident, police officers of the Municipal Public Security Bureau found a flower wreath left behind by the meeting at the Public Sports Ground, a large white cloth flag that read "Shanghai Citizens' United Association Against the Armistice Agreement and in Support of the Northeast Volunteers Commemorates the Martyrs Who Died Resisting Japan in Northeast China and Shanghai," many silk inspection, command, traffic, and various participating group flags, and various types of leaflets. At 1:00 PM, the police detachment of the Public Sports Ground began to withdraw, leaving only a few police officers from the Second District stationed to provide security and prevent further incidents.

Security measures were lifted at the borders of the Chinese and Concession areas. The evening was peaceful.

The Hurricane Is Blowing Northwards

Shanghai Fortunate to Escape Its Visit

The Shanghai Times reported: According to staff at the Xujiahui Observatory, the gusts of wind that blew through Shanghai yesterday (11th) afternoon and evening made many people apprehensive, fearing that the hurricane would visit Shanghai this morning (12th). Fortunately, later news of the hurricane indicated that it was still moving northward and would probably pass two hundred miles east of Shanghai today. (According to the Observatory's report on the evening of the 12th, the hurricane was lingering near Okinawa and had not moved north.) According to reports, this hurricane was caused by a low-pressure center that formed near Taiwan on Friday night. It blew across the East China Sea last night and moved north. This low-pressure area covers a wide range, encompassing the entire eastern part of China and the Yangtze River basin. However, the hurricane's trajectory has not shown any signs of shifting westward. The force of the hurricane is reportedly not particularly strong, and its movement is not very rapid. However, it is unusual for a hurricane to occur so early in the year.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: The northern part of the East China Sea has bad weather due to a low pressure that appears to be slowly moving northeast-east. Around Naha, the winds are still strong because the hurricane seems to have lingered and is gradually weakening. The Yangtze River estuary is overcast, and the Yangtze River basin is gradually clearing. Along the coast, the Taiwan Strait, and the Shandong coastline, there are localized areas of heavy fog. The center of the hurricane was within 120 miles of the intersection of 26 degrees north latitude and 126 degrees east longitude around 9:00 AM this morning and was moving very slowly, showing signs of lingering. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this area was 80.8 degrees and the lowest was 69.8 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 89.1 degrees and the lowest was 58.3 degrees.

Demands of Telephone Workers in the Concession

The Company Replied Yesterday

Unable to Accept the Basic Conditions

The Strike Committee Immediately Convened an Emergency Meeting

Yesterday was the sixth day of the telephone workers' strike in the concession. Automatic exchanges continued to operate as normal. The strike committee expanded its organization, and the situation remained serious. The company replied to the 14 demands made by the workers yesterday, stating that it could not accept them. All the workers felt that the company was insincere and convened a temporary emergency meeting that evening to discuss the course of action. The situation is described in detail below:

Police Notification: Yesterday was Sunday. The main office of the telephone company on Jiangxi Road and the branches in various districts were closed, and senior foreign staff stopped working as usual. However, the police had been ordered to send Chinese constables to guard the entrance of the company to provide protection. The Political Department of the General Police Station of the Public Concession specially sent Detective Zhang Yingmei to the contact point of the telephone workers' strike committee at the Commercial Hotel on Avenue Edouard VII to state that West Superintendent had instructed that the company's response to the workers' demands had been translated and requested that representatives be sent to the New Central Bank on Fujian Road at 2:00 PM for negotiations.

Company Response: After the strike committee received the police notification, they sent representatives Zheng Luojie, Weng Zhenhua, Xu Ruze, and Pan Dingquan at 2:00 PM.

Page 10

At the time, Company Engineer Harrison refuted the demands raised by the workers and, after the company had translated the English version and considered them, stated that they could not be accepted. This strike was actually instigated by a few troublemakers. It was hoped that they would resume work first. Thereupon, the representatives believed that the company was too insincere in negotiating and left together.

Company Announcement: The Shanghai Telephone Company's announcement to all workers stated: On June 9th, the Shanghai Telephone Company received two documents from the Shanghai Telephone Company Workers' Strike Committee, one of which contained the reasons for the current workers' strike (1) The company did not reward the workers for continuing to work during the Sino-Japanese War; (2) The company cancelled Sunday work and the wage increase regulations in April; (3) The company did not compensate for the dismissal of a large number of workers and denied

workers the right to participate in pensions, which had been confiscated; (4) The company plans to hire White Russians to replace Chinese workers. It is claimed that because of the above reasons, the workers began a strike at 7:00 PM on June 7th. However, it should be noted that the company was not notified in advance. It also stated that due to the above reasons, the workers abandoned public convenience and stopped working, and now they have made various demands. Regarding the above accusations against the company, the answers are as follows: (A) (1) The company continued to pay the full wages to many workers who were unable to work due to the war; (2) When the war broke out, the company paid workers double the amount of overtime pay; (3) The company provided many workers with free food; (4) The company accommodated many workers and their families to avoid the war. (B) (1) Due to the company's internal reorganization plan, Sunday overtime pay was greatly reduced; (2) Due to business reasons, the wages of workers in April were not increased. (C) As for the company's dismissal of workers, it was because the reorganization plan was in progress. However, the company paid pensions in accordance with the regulations, and in addition, they received more than the company was supposed to pay. (D) The company has not hired White Russians to replace Chinese workers, and there are no such plans to date. The company cannot recognize the union and does not want to handle any matters related to the union and the company through the union. Your workers are obviously being fooled by bad elements. Many of the demands are completely unacceptable. Some of them have nothing to do with the workers who have left their jobs, and the rest are untrue. The workers' strike this time disregards public convenience, and they did not give prior notice. It is dereliction of duty to the public. Moreover, during the strike, they also tried to destroy the machines, intending to cut off communications. The blame for disrupting the public is not slight. The company does not believe that the workers express sympathy for this kind of behavior. It only wants to think that this matter is entirely the work of a few instigators, and that the entire body of workers does not approve of this action. The company believes that all workers have been fooled, and after receiving this announcement, they will definitely realize and will no longer sympathize with the agitators' movement. Therefore, it is advised that all workers immediately resume work. The company is very willing to meet with the workers and discuss any issues raised by the workers in accordance with the company's procedures. The company's manager is also very happy to discuss with the workers various issues concerning the workers, and to accept and modify various feasible and reasonable methods. However, the twelve striking workers in the four districts who damaged the machines will be dismissed.

Shanghai Telephone Company, 11 June 1932.

Emergency Meeting: After the representatives withdrew, they reported to the strike committee. The chairman of the strike committee was immediately convened to discuss how to deal with the company. It was decided to convene a temporary emergency meeting at 9:30 PM that afternoon, and the documentation group rushed to issue an emergency notice, urging all members to attend in order to discuss concrete ways to deal with the company and the future course of action.

Workers' Statement: Yesterday, the striking workers in various district branches and warehouses of the telephone company held separate meetings on the order of the strike committee to discuss ways to intensify their work, improve the small group organization, establish a discipline enforcement task force, strictly guard against those who undermine strike discipline, establish fundraising teams in each industry, create flags and donation books, and prepare to go out and raise donations. Also, a reporter from the New Sound News Agency met with a member of the strike committee yesterday. According to the company's reply to our demands, the text is simple and can be said to be a rejection letter. Our basic conditions were completely rejected. Such oppression is hateful. Now all the workers have decided to discuss the second step of dealing with it.

Japanese Newspaper Report

Reasons for Song Ziwen's Resignation

The Opium Monopoly Plan Failed

But His Confidants Tried Hard to Implement It

According to the Japanese newspaper Shanghai Mainichi Shinbun published on the 12th, Song Ziwen resigned because the central government's finances were exhausted and the funds for the communist suppression had not been settled. He had contacted local financial groups for loans but to no avail. He was furious and resigned. Wang Jingwei came to Shanghai to persuade him to stay, but Song has not yet expressed any news of returning to office. However, according to reliable sources, Song has been trying to implement the opium monopoly plan, which was proposed last year but failed. His confidants Zhang Shouyong and Tang Haian are trying hard to implement the monopoly plan, which is still being implemented according to the plan set last year. A general bureau will be established in Nanjing, and branch bureaus will be established in Shanghai, Nanjing, Shanghai-Hangzhou lines, Wuhu, Anqing, Jiujiang and other ports, gradually extending to the five provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Fujian. It is estimated that the annual tax revenue can reach 200 million yuan, that is, even in Shanghai alone, it can

yield five or six million yuan per month.

Management Committee for Wounded Soldiers Ends

Since the January 28th Incident, the 19th Route Army and the 5th Army, fighting the Japanese in bloody battles for several months, have seen many of our loyal soldiers wounded by enemy artillery shells, bombs, machine guns and other military weapons. The people of Shanghai enthusiastically provided relief and established more than seventy wounded soldier hospitals. Doctors, male and female students from various schools, and famous ladies volunteered to go to the hospitals to diagnose and care for the wounded soldiers, tireless in their efforts, their enthusiasm is especially admirable. The Shanghai Office of the General Headquarters of the 19th Route Army also established a Management Committee for Wounded Soldiers in Shanghai at that time, sending Chief of Staff Zhan Baoguang of the General Headquarters as the chairman, and jointly organizing it with personnel dispatched by the various divisions of the 19th Army and the 5th Army. It has been over three months since its establishment. Now more than 90% of the wounded officers and soldiers have recovered and returned to their units. At present, there are only a few hundred seriously wounded and disabled soldiers left, so the Management Committee does not need to be established for a long time. It has been ordered to end immediately, and all unfinished matters after the end have been handed over to the personnel sent by each division for direct handling. The personnel sent by each division to take over the association are: Yu Huixun, adjutant of the 60th Division, Lin Ziyu, adjutant of the 61st Division, Zhang Baoying, adjutant of the 78th Division, and the 87th and 88th Divisions are managed by the Shanghai Office of the 5th Army. They are now continuing to be responsible for managing the wounded officers and soldiers of their respective divisions.

Comrades from Sichuan Who Went to Shanghai to Assist Arrived Yesterday

More than ten comrades who graduated from the Sichuan Student Volunteer Army Training Class of the 19th Route Army arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning by train from Wuxi and are now staying at the Datong Hotel. According to them, their mission to Shanghai is to investigate the situation after the Battle of Shanghai.

in order to inform their elders in Sichuan, and at the same time contact the Sichuan Fellow Villagers Association to provide economic assistance and borrow land to organize a lecture tour back to Sichuan to expand anti-Japanese propaganda and jointly save the crisis. The organizational outline of the 19th Route Army Student Volunteer Army Return

Sichuan Lecture Tour is as follows: (1) General Outline: Seeing that the Student Volunteer Army training has been completed and the Shanghai war has stopped, Sichuan is located in the remote west, and most of the people are not clear about the Shanghai war situation and the experience of going to Shanghai to assist, so there is a motive for organizing a lecture tour. (2) Purpose: The purpose of this group is to awaken the people, jointly save the crisis, and at the same time report on the tragic situation of the victims, the Shanghai war situation, and the experience of this group going to Shanghai to assist. (3) Name: This group is composed of more than ten Sichuan comrades who graduated from the Student Volunteer Army Training Class of the 19th Route Army, so it is named the 19th Route Army Student Volunteer Army Return Sichuan Lecture Tour. (4) Organization: Propaganda Group, with one director and several propagandists; Entertainment Group, with one director and several artists; General Affairs Group, with one director, two clerks, two liaison officers, and one accountant. (5) Expenses: The expenses of this group are temporarily shared by the members, and if there is not enough, they can be freely donated by the people's groups. (6) Supplementary Provisions: This outline will be implemented after it is passed by the founding meeting, and if there are any unfinished matters, it can be modified at any time. Initiators: Sun Yongyi, Wang Chuheng, Wei Yong, Yang Shaojian, He Chaoran, Li Bogong, Longquan, Huang Daoyuan.
